= 0.1387*(P²/8.038 - P - P³/(8.038·70.018) + P²/70.018)

**Second term:** 0.1387*(1 - P/70.018)*P
= 0.1387*P - 0.1387*P²/70.018

**Third term:** 0.1387*P/(1 + exp(-8.038*(P - 0.5894)))

Let me combine the polynomial parts (terms 1 and 2):
- P³ coefficient: -0.1387/(8.038·70.018)
- P² coefficient: 0.1387/8.038 + 0.1387/70.018 - 0.1387/70.018 = 0.1387/8.038
- P coefficient: -0.1387 + 0.1387 = 0
- Plus the sigmoid term: 0.1387*P/(1 + exp(-8.038*(P-0.5894)))
